\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Copyright\ (c)\ Electronic\ Arts\ Inc.\ All\ rights\ reserved.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ An\ slist\ is\ a\ singly-\/linked\ list.\ The\ C++\ standard\ library\ doesn't\ define}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ such\ a\ thing\ as\ an\ slist,\ nor\ does\ the\ C++\ TR1.\ Our\ implementation\ of\ slist}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ largely\ follows\ the\ design\ of\ the\ SGI\ STL\ slist\ container,\ which\ is\ also\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ found\ in\ STLPort.\ Singly-\/linked\ lists\ use\ less\ memory\ than\ doubly-\/linked\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ lists,\ but\ are\ less\ flexible.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ In\ looking\ at\ slist,\ you\ will\ notice\ a\ lot\ of\ references\ to\ things\ like}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 'before\ first',\ 'before\ last',\ 'insert\ after',\ and\ 'erase\ after'.\ This\ is\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ due\ to\ the\ fact\ that\ std::list\ insert\ and\ erase\ works\ on\ the\ node\ before}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ referenced\ node,\ whereas\ slist\ is\ singly\ linked\ and\ operations\ are\ only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ efficient\ if\ they\ work\ on\ the\ node\ after\ the\ referenced\ node.\ This\ is\ because}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ with\ an\ slist\ node\ you\ know\ the\ node\ after\ it\ but\ not\ the\ node\ before\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
